192{
193 if (!target)
194 return;

205 // UPDATETYPE_CREATE_OBJECT2 dynamic objects, corpses...
206 if (isType(TYPEMASK_DYNAMICOBJECT) || isType(TYPEMASK_CORPSE) || isType(TYPEMASK_PLAYER))

212

218 case GAMEOBJECT_TYPE_TRAP:
219 case GAMEOBJECT_TYPE_DUEL_ARBITER:
